## AI: Analysis

**Count**: 16 endpoints | **Tier**: LLM Inference | **Credits**: 10 per call

> **LLM Category Note**: These endpoints are expected to perform real Claude/GPT/Grok/DeepSeek inference, not template-based responses. Acceptable results require coherent, contextual output addressing the specific input. Known issue: timeouts on complex prompts exceeding 15 seconds.

| Slug | Expected Input | Expected Output | Acceptable Result | Computation Type | Outstanding Issues |

## Text Processing

**Count**: 90 endpoints | **Tier**: Mixed | **Credits**: 1 per call

| Slug | Expected Input | Expected Output | Acceptable Result | Computation Type | Outstanding Issues |

## Summary Statistics

- **Total endpoints documented**: 1255
- **Total categories**: 78
- **LLM inference categories**: 6
- **LLM endpoints**: 92
- **Compute/utility endpoints**: 1163

## Global Notes

### LLM Endpoints
- **Expected behavior**: Real Claude/GPT/Grok/DeepSeek inference, NOT template-based responses
- **Acceptable result**: Coherent response addressing the specific input with proper JSON structure
- **Known issue**: Timeouts on complex prompts exceeding 15 seconds
- **Provider selection**: Many LLM endpoints accept `provider=grok|deepseek|openai|anthropic` to select model
- **Credits**: Typically 10 credits per LLM call

### Compute Endpoints
- **Expected behavior**: Deterministic server-side computation
- **Acceptable result**: Correct result matching the documented output schema exactly
- **Credits**: Typically 1 credit per compute call

### External Endpoints
- **Expected behavior**: Proxy or enriched call to third-party APIs
- **Acceptable result**: Valid response from upstream; graceful degradation on service unavailability
- **Credits**: Varies by endpoint
